 artiai kanoon ke tahat soochna ayog un sthitiyon main logon kii shikayaton or apil par faisla karte hai jab ve iske vibhinn praavdhaanon ke tahat suchanaaen hasil karne main naakaam rahete hai
 Under the RTI Act, 2005, Information Commissioners enjoyed both tenure protection and high status and this gave them the right to function autonomously
 isaki badaulat ve desh ke sarvocch padon par asin logon ko bhi suchanaaen dene kaa nirdesh de sakate hai
 The commissioners had a fixed tenure of five years (retirement age is fixed at 65 years) and the salaries, allowances and other service conditions of the Commissioners of the Central Information Commission and the heads of the State Information Commission were at par with the Election Commissioners
